You can say Redial, Call History or Dial Number For help with other modes, say more help after the beep. There are 5 tutorials to use voice recognition. Tutorial 1. Starting the voice recognition session. To start the voice recognition session, press the push to talk button on the steering wheel and say your command after the beep. To interrupt a voice prompt, press the push to talk button and wait until you hear the beep before saying your next command. If you want to end the voice session, you can press and hold the push to talk button until you hear the double beep that signifies the end of the session or you can say cancel at any time. That s the end of the first tutorial. Tutorial 2. Blue tooth connection. In order for hands free calling to work in the vehicle, Blue tooth has to be enabled from your mobile phone. Enabling Blue tooth is different for each phone, but you can usually find this in your phone s setup menu. If you need additional help, please consult your phone .hyundaiusa.com/Blue tooth" for a list of Blue tooth compatible devices. That s the end of the second tutorial. Tutorial 5. Improving the voice recognition environment. Improving the voice recognition environment involves reducing cabin and background noise. Please make sure that the windows are closed, the air conditioner fan is set to low, and that background noise such as other conversations are minimized. That s the end of the fifth tutorial. Tutorial 3. How to find available voice commands. Voice recognition works by playing a beep and then waiting for a spoken command. The command must be said after the beep has finished playing. A few sample commands are radio, and call. A detailed list of available commands in each mode can be found by saying help and then more help. They can also be found in the vehicle s user manual.
